2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

## Your Task

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the security domain.

43-assistanttext-
The answer has been written to `/workspace/answer.json`. Here's a summary of the findings:

## API Key Authentication & Scope Enforcement in Grafana

### Core Authentication Client
**`pkg/services/authn/clients/api_key.go`** — The central file. Key functions:
- `Authenticate` — extracts token from `Authorization` header, validates it
- `validateApiKey` — enforces expiration, revocation, org-scoping, and service-account linkage
- `getFromToken` / `getFromTokenLegacy` — handles both modern (satokengen) and legacy (HMAC) key formats
- `Hook` — post-auth hook to update `last_used_at`

### Middleware
**`pkg/services/contexthandler/contexthandler.go`** — HTTP middleware (`ContextHandler.Middleware`) that orchestrates all authn clients including API key auth. Puts the authenticated identity into the request context.

### API Key Service & Storage
- **`pkg/services/apikey/apikey.go`** — `Service` interface (`GetAPIKeyByHash`, `GetApiKeyByName`, `UpdateAPIKeyLastUsedDate`, etc.)
- **`pkg/services/apikey/model.go`** — `APIKey` model with `Expires`, `IsRevoked`, `ServiceAccountId` fields
- **`pkg/services/apikey/apikeyimpl/apikey.go`** — Service implementation
- **`pkg/services/apikey/apikeyimpl/xorm_store.go`** — SQL store (hash lookup, expiry storage, last-used update)

### gRPC Scope Enforcement
**`pkg/services/grpcserver/interceptors/auth.go`** — gRPC-layer authenticator that additionally enforces `org.RoleAdmin` role and loads RBAC permissions via `AccessControlService`.

The `APIKey` struct implements `authn.ContextAwareClient` and `authn.HookClient`. The `Authenticate` method extracts the token from the HTTP `Authorization` header (Bearer or Basic with username `api_key`), looks it up via the apikey service, and calls `validateApiKey` to enforce key validity. `validateApiKey` checks: (a) key expiration (`errAPIKeyExpired`), (b) revocation status (`errAPIKeyRevoked`), (c) organization mismatch (`errAPIKeyOrgMismatch`), and (d) that the key is linked to a service account (plain API keys without service accounts are rejected as `errAPIKeyInvalid`). **pkg/services/authn/clients/api_key.go** \u2014 The primary API key authentication client. The `APIKey` struct implements `authn.ContextAwareClient` and `authn.HookClient`. The `Authenticate` method extracts the token from the HTTP `Authorization` header (Bearer or Basic with username `api_key`), looks it up via the apikey service, and calls `validateApiKey` to enforce key validity. `validateApiKey` checks: (a) key expiration (`errAPIKeyExpired`), (b) revocation status (`errAPIKeyRevoked`), (c) organization mismatch (`errAPIKeyOrgMismatch`), and (d) that the key is linked to a service account (plain API keys without service accounts are rejected as `errAPIKeyInvalid`). Both legacy (HMAC-based) and modern (satokengen-prefixed) token formats are supported via `getFromTokenLegacy` and `getFromToken`.\\n\\n2. **pkg/services/contexthandler/contexthandler.go** \u2014 The HTTP middleware (`ContextHandler.Middleware`) that initializes the request context. It calls `h.authenticator.Authenticate`, which dispatches to the registered authn clients (including `APIKey`). On success, the signed-in user is placed in the context. The `authenticator.getSignedInUser` method validates a Bearer token by hash, fetches the associated service account, enforces `org.RoleAdmin` role requirement (scope enforcement for gRPC), and checks that the service account is not disabled. Permissions are loaded via `AccessControlService.GetUserPermissions`.\\n\\n9. **pkg/services/authn/authn.go** \u2014 Defines `ClientAPIKey = \\\"auth.client.api-key\\\"` constant and the `authn.Request`/`authn.Identity` types used throughout the auth flow.\\n\\n10. **pkg/services/authn/authnimpl/registration.go** \u2014 Registers the `APIKey` client with the authn service via `authnSvc.RegisterClient(clients.ProvideAPIKey(apikeyService, tracer))`.\"\n}\n",
